Its the perfect place to go! When it comes to celebrations they have everything! What I love most about it is that they have a giant variety of things. When you walk in you whats in store for the next holiday from Easter to Halloween and much more. They also have sunglasses and School supplies! Also they is wrapping paper, balloons, cards and envelopes for them. Then even better they have the table wrap. You can also get snacks there! They have food! They have a ton of sweets and great things that everyone can benefit from.They even have foam plates to have the food on. They also have canned food and plastic utensils. They also have laundry detergents. They even have air wicks to make your home smell amazing. The best part? Its all a dollar.</Review>

< Review>
I am going to give them a solid 4 Stars. I just happened to be off Convoy and the 52, so I let maps choose lunch/dinner for me, good old Gualbertos came up first. Now I am not sure who did their marketing or if its any way related but what sealed the deal was the Italian Bakery Chef on the the signage out front. I was the only one here about 5:15pm, Ordered the Carne Asada Burrito with cheese and maybe 5 minutes had the burrito in hand. First thing, went to my car and checked the meat. Yeah baby NO burnt meat, I am living the dream.
Burrito tasted good, will definitely come again and try something different, staff speak English possible second language so a little bit of a barrier here, and unfortunately no drive thru. Bit overall recommend you give them a chance for sure.</Review>

< review>
I work close by and this place is pretty good. Its a little taco shop in a strip mall, nothing fancy but clean with several tables. Their rolled tacos are what I normally get since its easy to eat at my desk at work. They are great and loaded with guacamole thats very flavorful with just the right amount of cheese.  I tried their shrimp burrito - comes with rice, cheese and sour cream. Mine had large shrimp that were cooked perfectly but I asked for very little rice and it had way too much for my liking - and I didnt taste any sour cream..?  The burrito was a generous size and the tortilla was soft and fresh, not soggy or hard like some other places.< /review>

<user>113321117875544945837<//user><user_name>Spencer Hom</user_name>< Time>
1521296614378</Time>
<rating>3< /rating>< review>
This is quite a small taco shop. The menu is pretty standard, they have just about everything. They have daily specials, which are about $1 off the regular price. I would say in general the prices seem a little too high, but the portion does seem to be more than enough.

I got the cheese enchilada combo. The enchiladas were okay, the sauce wasn't that flavorful with that deep red color. There was a lot of cheese inside, slightly melted but not a lot. The rice is yellow in color, but it did have flavor. The beans are smooth, but it has a taste that I cannot identify...probably some meat oil.

Overall, it's just okay here and is good for a quick meal.<//review>

I eat here a couple times a week. The food is always fast and fresh. I don't find it very expensive. They also have a daily happy hour menu with many items to choose from. They have a habenero salsa that's exceptionally hot, but it is labeled as such. It's rare to find a place that will actually make a hot salsa.  Many people are sensitive to HOT salsas. They do however have mild and medium choices. I have always recieved very good service here. They guy Dave who works the register isn't Mr. Cheerful, but he's nice, never rude and always provides great service. I like</Review>

<Text>Phenomenal event, so much information covering a very broad base of topics. Some of these topics were light on details due to time constraints, but even the overview gave me more to think about than Ive ever gotten at an event like this.

As a jumping-off point, I would highly recommend this. There are ways of searching for this information on your own, sure, but it would take an immense amount of time and you may end up missing certain topics because you may not even think to dig into them.

This is not going to be a one-shot, fully comprehensive seminar on all things real estate, thats simply unrealistic; rather it should be thought of as Real Estate 101.

There was some of the weekend devoted to discussing the value of continued study in their other programs, but thats expected for an event like this.</Text>< rating>

< Text>
The Fortune Builders 3 day seminar led by Jon Steingraber was excellent on all levels.  Jon was energetic, enthusiastic, transparent and he kept the seminar fast paced and interesting.  His authenticity and in depth knowledge of real estate investing and his grasp of the numbers that go with it was quite amazing and evident throughout.

The 3 day seminar was very informative and a good overview for someone like me who is new to real estate investing and just wanted to learn more about it and to understand how Fortune Builders operates and what they offer.  I loved the fact that Jon shared actual real properties in the surrounding areas that I am familiar with that could be looked up and actually seen.  No shenanigans whatsoever.

As I expected there is an upsell for the Fortune Builders Mastery programs which are very enticing and are of course a substantial investment as any decent business opportunity is.  I chose not to sign up for the Mastery programs at this time and at no time did I feel pressured by anyone to do so.

My overall impression of Fortune Builders and Jon is that they approach real estate investing professionally, properly, and with a high level of integrity and they offer a very solid, repeatable system to support people with real estate investing.  Just be sure it is right for you and that you are taking this on as a business and are strongly committed if you do choose to sign up for their Mastery program.</Text>
